This is the first Osage dictionary in the modern orthography =)
Each Osage word is written in the Osage alphabet and in a Latin transliteration
Can't see the Osage on your device? Download a font: https://www.google.com/get/noto/#sans-osge
This was not possible without the help of many volunteers
Thanks to Jakub, Wojtek, Filippos, Jonás, Victor, Aaron, Tahsin, Hubert, Christopher, Santiago, Max, and Batyah
Special thanks to Craig, Mark, Michele, and Aino!
I hope that this project will help people learn Osage so that the language can be passed onto future generations
-Harris

a, an	𐓷𐓣͘, 𐓷𐓣͘𐓸𐓲𐓟	wį, wįxce
abalone	𐓲𐓶𐓤𐓟	hcúke
abandon someone	𐓤𐓣𐓤𐓪𐓬𐓮𐓟, 𐓪𐓤𐓣𐓵𐓟	kihkoopse, ohkíðe
abdomen	𐓲𐓟𐓺𐓟, 𐓷𐓘𐓩𐓪͘𐓜𐓟𐓪ž𐓶	hcéze, wánǫbréoožú
abhor	𐓣𐓮𐓣	íisi
abnormal in appearance	𐓟ž𐓣𐓸𐓲𐓣 	éžixci

above: go, be, or place something ~	𐓘𐓨𐓘͘𐓯𐓣	ámąši

act unsuitably	𐓪𐓤'𐓘 𐓟ž𐓣 	ók'a eži
